1a1('bum): (kha) @#/ ! /sher phyin stong phrag brgya pa bzhugs so/ /
1a2('bum): (黃) 大般若經第二部
1b1('bum): @##/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa/ / bam po dang po/ /
1b2('bum): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor khyod kyis don gyi dbang gang zhig mthong na/
1b3('bum): de skad du gzugs kyang byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/ gzugs ma yin pa gzhan yang
1b4('bum): byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/ gzugs la yang byang chub sems dpa' yod pa ma yin/

1b7('bum): gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/ tshor ba la yang byang chub sems
1b8('bum): dpa' yod pa ma yin/ byang chub sems dpa' la yang tshor ba yod pa ma yin/

7b2('bum): de bzhin nyid yod pa ma yin/ ro'i de bzhin nyid med pa yang byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/ reg gi de bzhin nyid kyang byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/ reg gi de bzhin nyid ma yin pa gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/

9a1('bum): shes pa'i khams kyi de bzhin nyid kyang byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/ lce'i rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi de bzhin nyid ma yin pa gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/ lce'i rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi de

10a8('bum): yod pa ma yin/ rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi de bzhin nyid med pa yang byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/ ma rig pa'i de bzhin nyid kyang byang chub sems dpa' ma yin/ ma rig pa'i de bzhin nyid ma yin pa gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' ma

11b4('bum): gzugs ma lags pa gzhan byang chub sems dpar 'gyur ba lta yang ga la mchis/ gzugs la byang chub sems dpa' mchis par yang ga la 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' la gzugs mchis par yang ga la 'gyur/ gzugs
11b5('bum): ma mchis pa byang chub sems dpar 'gyur ba lta yang ga la mchis/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' shin tu ma mchis shing mi dmigs na/ de la tshor ba'i tshig bla dgas byang chub sems dpar 'gyur ba lta ga la mchis/

225a3('bum): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ thabs myi mkhas pas mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid myi rtag ces bgyi bar spyod na mtshan ma la spyod do/ /bcom ldan 'das gal te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes
225a4('bum): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ thabs myi mkhas pas mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid bde zhes bgyi bar spyod na mtshan ma la spyod do/ /bcom ldan 'das gal te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi
225a5('bum): pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ thabs myi mkhas pas mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid sdug bsngal zhes bgyi bar spyod na mtshan ma la spyod do/ /bcom ldan 'das gal te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab
